# This resource is a compilation of a mapping between Mandarin Chinese
# lemmas and their candidate classifiers to the Open Multilingual Wordnet,
# through Princeton Wordnet 3.0 synsets. Two files are made available:
# 1. (Raw, text-based) Chinese lemma mapping, with frequencies, to a list of 204 sortal classifiers 
# 2. Princeton Wordnet synset mapping, with frequencies, to a list of 204 sortal classifiers 
# The frequencies presented here are raw (i.e. no filtering was applied), refering to the dataset described
# as Tau=1, in the appended publication.
#
# Canonical Citation and description of this resource: 
# @inproceedings{Morgado:Bond:Gao:2016,
#   author    = {Morgado da Costa, Luís  and
#                Bond, Francis and
#                Gao, Helena},
#   title     = {Mapping and Generating Classifiers using an Open Chinese Ontology},
#   booktitle = {Proceedings of the 8th Global WordNet Conference (GWC 2016)},
#   address = {Bucharest, Romania},
#   year      = {2016}
# }
#
# License:
# Copyright (c) 2016 Luis Morgado da Costa (lmorgado.dacosta@gmail.com)
# Both files in this dataset (i.e. lemma and wordnet mappings) are released
# under a CC-BY-4.0 license (https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/);
#
# Data Format:
# ChineseLemma   \t   Classifier   \t   FrequencyCount
